It is the past practice of bodhisattvas and it is held by the bodhisattvas.” 
{{milestone:{label:13.3,id:UT22084-089-013-1338}}}Venerable Śāradvatīputra asked the Bhagavat, “Bhagavat, if a dhāraṇī is not located in an object and not located in a direction, then, Bhagavat, what is the meaning of the word dhāraṇī?”
{{milestone:{label:13.4,id:UT22084-089-013-1339}}}The Bhagavat replied to Venerable Śāradvatīputra, “Śāradvatīputra, you are within the Mahāyāna, have faith in the Mahāyāna, and are adept in the Mahāyāna. Śāradvatīputra, it is just you who have taught that a dhāraṇī is not located in an object and not located in a direction. It is not a phenomenon. It is not a nonphenomenon. It is not past, it is not future, and it is not present. It is not a thing, and it is not nothing. It does not originate from a condition, and it does not originate from the absence of a condition. It does not originate from a being, and it does not originate from the absence of a being.{{note:{index:278,id:UT22084-089-013-1340}}} It is not the production of any phenomenon, and it is not their cessation. 
{{milestone:{label:13.5,id:UT22084-089-013-1341}}}“Nevertheless, it is excellent, excellent, that, for the benefit of bodhisattvas, there is the teaching on the topic of the knowledge and power of the path of practicing the Dharma teaching of The Dhāraṇī of Nonattachment, which is composed of the qualities of the buddhas, the correct conduct of the buddhas, the training of the buddhas, the intention of the buddhas, and the occurrence of the buddhas.” {{page:{number:156,id:UT22084-089-013-3107,folio:F.229.a}}}
{{milestone:{label:13.6,id:UT22084-089-013-1342}}}Then Venerable Śāradvatīputra said to the Bhagavat, “Bhagavat, I pray that you give the Dharma teaching of the dhāraṇī. A bodhisattva who has obtained the dhāraṇī, wherever they dwell, will be irreversible from the highest, most complete enlightenment; their commitments will be genuine, they will be ācāryas with an eloquence that has the nature of being a nondependent phenomenon, and they will remain perfectly upon the path. I pray for the Sugata to teach it.” 
{{milestone:{label:13.7,id:UT22084-089-013-1343}}}The Bhagavat said to Śāradvatīputra, “Excellent, excellent, Śāradvatīputra! It is so. The bodhisattva who has obtained this dhāraṇī should be called a buddha. Śāradvatīputra, whoever honors, venerates, serves, and makes offerings to a bodhisattva who has obtained this dhāraṇī will be someone who has honored a buddha. 
{{milestone:{label:13.8,id:UT22084-089-013-1344}}}“Śāradvatīputra, anyone who hears this dhāraṇī, anyone who possesses this dhāraṇī, and anyone who aspires to this dhāraṇī will become inseparable from the enlightenment mind, the same as if they had made offerings to a buddha.
{{milestone:{label:13.9,id:UT22084-089-013-1345}}}“Śāradvatīputra, this is the dhāraṇī:
{{milestone:{label:13.10,id:UT22084-089-013-1346}}}tadyathā | sandhāraṇi utdhāraṇi susaṃpratiṣṭhite sunāma supratiṣṭhite vijayabala, sattyapratijñā suāroha jñānapratiutpādani avanāvani abhiṣiñcani abhivyāhāra{{note:{index:279,id:UT22084-089-013-1347}}} śubhavati suniḥśrita{{note:{index:280,id:UT22084-089-013-1348}}} bahuguṃbha abhivadā svāhā |
{{milestone:{label:13.11,id:UT22084-089-013-1349}}}“Śāradvatīputra, any bodhisattva who is firmly established in the words of this dhāraṇī of nonattachment perfectly retains them and possesses them, and so their prayer will not be exhausted for an eon, for longer than an eon,{{note:{index:281,id:UT22084-089-013-1350}}} for a thousand eons, or for a hundred thousand eons. {{page:{number:157,id:UT22084-089-013-3108,folio:F.229.b}}} Their body will not be harmed by weapons or poisons, and they will not be bitten by snakes. 
{{milestone:{label:13.12,id:UT22084-089-013-1351}}}“Why is that? Śāradvatīputra, it is because this unbounded dhāraṇī is the mother of the buddhas of the past, the mother of the buddhas of the future, and the mother of the buddhas of the present, and that is this Dharma teaching called The Dhāraṇī of Nonattachment.
{{milestone:{label:13.13,id:UT22084-089-013-1352}}}“Śāradvatīputra, if someone were to fill ten asaṃkhyeya trichiliocosm world realms with the seven jewels and make an offering of them to the buddha bhagavats, and if they were to provide the requisites of clothing and food of various kinds for asaṃkhyeya eons, the merit that comes from someone who possesses just one word of this dhāraṇī would still be far greater. 
{{milestone:{label:13.14,id:UT22084-089-013-1353}}}“Why is that? Śāradvatīputra, it is because this Dharma teaching of the unbounded dhāraṇī is the mother of the tathāgatas.”{{note:{index:282,id:UT22084-089-013-1354}}}
{{milestone:{label:13.15,id:UT22084-089-013-1355}}}This concludes “The Dhāraṇī of Nonattachment,” the thirteenth chapter of “The Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light.”
{{milestone:{label:14,id:UT22084-089-013-chapter-14}}}Chapter 14: The Wish-fulfilling Jewel Dhāraṇī 
{{milestone:{label:14.1,id:UT22084-089-013-1357}}}Then the Bhagavat, in the midst of the great assembly, said to Venerable Ānanda, “Ānanda, there is that which repels all lightning, which has been taught by the samyaksaṃbuddhas of the past. Following them, I also will now teach it, so you should retain it! 
{{milestone:{label:14.2,id:UT22084-089-013-1358}}}“Ānanda, to the east there is the lightning called Āgata, to the south there is the lightning called Hundredth Moment, to the west there is the lightning called Waning Light, and to the north there is the lightning called Satamapati. 
{{milestone:{label:14.3,id:UT22084-089-013-1359}}}“Ānanda, someone who knows the name of each lightning and knows the direction where it is situated {{page:{number:158,id:UT22084-089-013-3109,folio:F.230.a}}} will know that all danger from lightning will not occur. When they write down the names of the lightning, wherever they dwell there will be no lightning that strikes.”
{{milestone:{label:14.4,id:UT22084-089-013-1360}}}Then, at that time, the Bhagavat recited these words of a Dravidian mantra:
{{milestone:{label:14.5,id:UT22084-089-013-1361}}}tadyathā | nimi nimi nimindhari, illuminator of the three worlds who holds a trident in his hands, protect me, protect me from all lightning in this place! svāhā |{{note:{index:283,id:UT22084-089-013-1362}}}
{{milestone:{label:14.6,id:UT22084-089-013-1363}}}Also at that time, the bodhisattva mahāsattva Avalokiteśvara was present in that assembly. Being present, he said to the Bhagavat, “Bhagavat, I also, for this Dharma teaching, will recite the words of a Dravidian mantra:
{{milestone:{label:14.7,id:UT22084-089-013-1364}}}tadyathā | kate vikate nikate pratyarthike pratyamitre śuddhe mukte vimale prabhāsvare aṇḍare paṇḍare śvete paṇḍaravāsini harikaṇḍari piṃgala{{note:{index:284,id:UT22084-089-013-1365}}} akṣi dadhi mukhi. Protect me, protect me from all premature death. Through the magnificence of Ārya Avalokiteśvara may I never see any premature death! svāhā |{{note:{index:285,id:UT22084-089-013-1366}}}
{{milestone:{label:14.8,id:UT22084-089-013-1367}}}Then Vajrapāṇi, the lord of secrets, placed his palms together, bowed toward the Bhagavat, and said to the Bhagavat, “Bhagavat, I also will recite the words of a dhāraṇī for this Dharma teaching:
{{milestone:{label:14.9,id:UT22084-089-013-1368}}}tadyathā | muni muni muni nadhari muni mati mati sumati mahāmati hā hā hā hā. Vajrapāṇi has said, ‘You have no bad karma, so do not be afraid!’ svāhā |{{note:{index:286,id:UT22084-089-013-1369}}}
{{milestone:{label:14.10,id:UT22084-089-013-1370}}}“Bhagavat, whoever keeps in their heart this invincible protection of mine, or writes it out, will always be continually protected from all danger. I will save them from all premature death.” {{page:{number:159,id:UT22084-089-013-3110,folio:F.230.b}}}
{{milestone:{label:14.11,id:UT22084-089-013-1371}}}Then Mahābrahmā, the lord of Sahā, said to the Bhagavat, “Bhagavat, I also, for the welfare, benefit, and happiness of beings, will recite the words of a mantra for this Dharma teaching: 
{{milestone:{label:14.12,id:UT22084-089-013-1372}}}tadyathā | hili mili cili svāhā brahmapūre svāha brahmasvare svāha brahmabhisugarbhe puṣpasaṃstare svāhā |
{{milestone:{label:14.13,id:UT22084-089-013-1373}}}“Bhagavat, this protection of mine is called Brahmā’s punishment, and it will protect from all premature death and bring to an end all bad karma.”
{{milestone:{label:14.14,id:UT22084-089-013-1374}}}Then Śakra, the lord of devas, with his palms together, bowed toward the Bhagavat and said to the Bhagavat, “Bhagavat, I also will recite the words of a dhāraṇī-mantra for this Dharma teaching:
{{milestone:{label:14.15,id:UT22084-089-013-1375}}}tadyathā | nivarāni banddha mādantema titi titi gaurī gandhari caṇḍāli mātaṅgi{{note:{index:287,id:UT22084-089-013-1376}}} parṇale{{note:{index:288,id:UT22084-089-013-1377}}} hinamadhyamadhariṇi malani dalamdade{{note:{index:289,id:UT22084-089-013-1378}}} cakrāvākrī{{note:{index:290,id:UT22084-089-013-1379}}} śavari savari svāhā |
{{milestone:{label:14.16,id:UT22084-089-013-1380}}}“Venerable Bhagavat, this vidyāmantra of mine, which is called hurled-down vajra flames,{{note:{index:291,id:UT22084-089-013-1381}}} frees from all dangers, all fear and terror, and protects from all premature death.”
{{milestone:{label:14.17,id:UT22084-089-013-1382}}}Then Mahārāja Dhṛtarāṣṭra, Mahārāja Virūḍhaka, Mahārāja Virūpākṣa, and Mahārāja Vaiśravaṇa bowed toward the Bhagavat, and said to the Bhagavat, “Bhagavat, we also, in order to bring benefit to many beings, in order to bring happiness to many beings, {{page:{number:160,id:UT22084-089-013-3111,folio:F.231.a}}} and because of compassion for the world, will recite the words of a mantra for this Dharma teaching:
{{milestone:{label:14.18,id:UT22084-089-013-1383}}}tadyathā | puṣpe supuṣpe dhumaparihāre āryapraśaste{{note:{index:292,id:UT22084-089-013-1384}}} śānti nirmukte maṅgalya{{note:{index:293,id:UT22084-089-013-1385}}} hiraṇyagarbhe stute stavite svāhā |
{{milestone:{label:14.19,id:UT22084-089-013-1386}}}“Venerable Bhagavat, this protection of ours, of we Four Mahārājas, which is called the absence of danger, makes those in danger become safe, protects life, and saves from all premature death.” 
{{milestone:{label:14.20,id:UT22084-089-013-1387}}}Then the nāga king Sāgara, the nāga king Vidyutprabha, the nāga king Anavatapta, the nāga king Lightning Tongue, and the nāga king Royal Light, with palms together, bowed toward the Bhagavat and said to the Bhagavat, “Bhagavat, our great protection, which is called the wish-fulfilling jewel, repels all lightning, prevents all premature death, neutralizes poisons, and causes danger from enemies, conjured spirits, zombies, and inauspiciousness to cease. 
{{milestone:{label:14.21,id:UT22084-089-013-1388}}}“Bhagavat, regard us with compassion and accept this, so that we may leave this existence as nāgas and forsake miserliness. Why is that? Bhagavat we nāgas are miserly, and our minds are encircled by miserliness. 
{{milestone:{label:14.22,id:UT22084-089-013-1389}}}tadyathā | āryaje{{note:{index:294,id:UT22084-089-013-1390}}} amare amṛte akṣaye abhiye puṇyai paryavate{{note:{index:295,id:UT22084-089-013-1391}}} sarvapāpaṃ praśamāniye svāha āryapuṇyasopākiye{{note:{index:296,id:UT22084-089-013-1392}}} svāhā |
{{milestone:{label:14.23,id:UT22084-089-013-1393}}}“Venerable Bhagavat, if any man or woman recites the words of this mantra with their tongue or writes it out, then they will know that there is no danger from lightning and there will be no premature death caused by poison from plants, poison from animal bites, {{page:{number:161,id:UT22084-089-013-3112,folio:F.231.b}}} poison from treasures, or any other category of poison. May I go from all dangers and all harm to become perfectly happy!” 
{{milestone:{label:14.24,id:UT22084-089-013-1394}}}The Bhagavat then congratulated Śakra, Brahmā, the world protectors, and the nāga lords, saying, “It is excellent, excellent that you elegant men have taught the words of the Dravidian mantras in order to enter and possess completely this Dharma teaching, for the sake of benefit for many beings and happiness for many beings. It will protect in every direction those who are asleep, those who are intoxicated, and even those who are completely intoxicated.”
{{milestone:{label:14.25,id:UT22084-089-013-1395}}}Then the Bhagavat said to the great assembly, “Well done! Well done! All of these dhāraṇī-mantras have great power, so that all the things wished for in the minds of beings will be perfectly obtained, exactly as they have wanted. They will bring a vast benefit as long as the mind is one-pointed. Do not have any doubt!”
{{milestone:{label:14.26,id:UT22084-089-013-1396}}}When the Bhagavat had spoken, the world, with its bhikṣus, Śakra, Brahmā, world protectors, nāga lords, devas, humans, asuras, and gandharvas, was overjoyed and praised the words of the Bhagavat.
{{milestone:{label:14.27,id:UT22084-089-013-1397}}}This concludes “The Wish-Fulfilling Jewel Dhāraṇī,” the fourteenth chapter of “The Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light.”
{{milestone:{label:15,id:UT22084-089-013-chapter-15}}}Chapter 15: The Goddess Sarasvatī
{{milestone:{label:15.1,id:UT22084-089-013-1399}}}Then the great goddess Sarasvatī, with her robe over one shoulder, kneeling with her right knee on the ground and her palms together in homage, bowed toward the Bhagavat and said to the Bhagavat, “Venerable Bhagavat, I, the great goddess Sarasvatī, will bring eloquence to the words of those dharmabhāṇakas so that their words will be beautified. I will also bestow on them the power of mental retention. I will establish them in giving definitions. I will illuminate those dharmabhāṇakas with the great light of knowledge.{{note:{index:297,id:UT22084-089-013-1400}}} If any line of verse or syllables of this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light is left out, or forgotten, {{page:{number:162,id:UT22084-089-013-3113,folio:F.232.a}}} I will bring all definitions, lines of verse, and syllables to those dharmabhāṇaka bhikṣus.
{{milestone:{label:15.2,id:UT22084-089-013-1402}}}“So that{{note:{index:298,id:UT22084-089-013-1403}}} this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light may remain for a long time in Jambudvīpa and not quickly vanish; so that beings can accomplish roots of merit with a hundred thousand buddha bhagavats; so that many beings on hearing this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light may develop inconceivably sharp wisdom; so that they may gain an inconceivable aggregation of wisdom;{{note:{index:299,id:UT22084-089-013-1404}}} so that they may attain good fortune in this life; so that they may have benefit in life and possess an immeasurable aggregation of merit; so that they may seek a variety of methods;{{note:{index:300,id:UT22084-089-013-1405}}} so that they may become learned{{note:{index:301,id:UT22084-089-013-1406}}} in all treatises; and so that they may attain{{note:{index:302,id:UT22084-089-013-1407}}} perfection{{note:{index:303,id:UT22084-089-013-1408}}} in a variety of arts, I will bestow the power of retention so that they will not forget.{{note:{index:304,id:UT22084-089-013-1401}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.3,id:UT22084-089-013-1409}}}“I will teach the rite of cleansing with mantras and medicines for the benefit of the dharmabhāṇaka bhikṣus and the beings who listen to the Dharma, so that harm from the planets, lunar asterisms, birth, and death; all the harms from fighting, pollution, riots, chaos, nightmares, and misleaders; and the harms from all evil spirits and vetālas will cease.
{{milestone:{label:15.4,id:UT22084-089-013-1410}}}“These are the herbs and medicines through which the wise can cleanse themselves:
{{milestone:{label:15.5,id:UT22084-089-013-1411}}}“Sweet flag, cow bezoar, and fenugreek,
Artemisia, acacia, and shami,{{note:{index:305,id:UT22084-089-013-1412}}}
Orris root and musk,{{note:{index:306,id:UT22084-089-013-1413}}}
Crepe ginger, cinnamon, and agarwood;
{{milestone:{label:15.6,id:UT22084-089-013-1414}}}“Chir pine rosin and dammar gum, 
Bdellium and frankincense, 
Valerian and black stone flower, 
Sandalwood and realgar; {{page:{number:163,id:UT22084-089-013-3114,folio:F.232.b}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.7,id:UT22084-089-013-1415}}}“Bezoar{{note:{index:307,id:UT22084-089-013-1416}}} and costus root, 
Saffron, nut grass, and mustard seed, 
Linseed, cardamom, and spikenard, 
And ironwood flowers and vetiver:
{{milestone:{label:15.8,id:UT22084-089-013-1417}}}“Combine equal amounts of each
During the Puṣya lunar house.
Recite these mantra words
A hundred times over the powder:
{{milestone:{label:15.9,id:UT22084-089-013-1418}}}tadyathā | sute kṛte{{note:{index:308,id:UT22084-089-013-1419}}} kamatali nalejanakarate{{note:{index:309,id:UT22084-089-013-1420}}} haṅkarate{{note:{index:310,id:UT22084-089-013-1421}}} indrajalini{{note:{index:311,id:UT22084-089-013-1422}}} śaṃkaradri{{note:{index:312,id:UT22084-089-013-1423}}} paśaddre{{note:{index:313,id:UT22084-089-013-1424}}} avartakaseke{{note:{index:314,id:UT22084-089-013-1425}}} nakutra kukavilakavimalamati śīlamati{{note:{index:315,id:UT22084-089-013-1426}}} sandhidhudhumamavati śiśiri satyasthite{{note:{index:316,id:UT22084-089-013-1427}}} svāhā |{{note:{index:317,id:UT22084-089-013-1428}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.10,id:UT22084-089-013-1429}}}“Make a circle of cow dung
And scatter flower petals.
Pour sweetened water
Into a gold bowl and a silver bowl.
{{milestone:{label:15.11,id:UT22084-089-013-1430}}}“You should also place there
Four men dressed in armor,
And place there four maidens
Who are adorned and holding pots.
{{milestone:{label:15.12,id:UT22084-089-013-1431}}}“Perfume the air with bdellium
And play the five kinds of musical instruments.{{note:{index:318,id:UT22084-089-013-1432}}}
Adorn the goddess with 
Banners, parasols, and flags.
{{milestone:{label:15.13,id:UT22084-089-013-1433}}}“In between, place mirrors
And arrange arrows and spears.
Then, after closing the boundary,
Commence what is to be done.
{{milestone:{label:15.14,id:UT22084-089-013-1434}}}syād yathedaṃ{{note:{index:319,id:UT22084-089-013-1435}}} arake nayane hile mile gile khikhile svāhā |{{note:{index:320,id:UT22084-089-013-1436}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.15,id:UT22084-089-013-1437}}}“Engage in the peaceful activity of cleansing by reciting this mantra while washing the body of the Bhagavat: 
{{milestone:{label:15.16,id:UT22084-089-013-1438}}}tadyathā | sugaṭe vigaṭe vigatāvati svāhā |{{note:{index:321,id:UT22084-089-013-1439}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.17,id:UT22084-089-013-1440}}}“May the lunar asterisms, wherever they are 
In the four directions, protect lives.
May they bring to an end the dreadful terrors
Of the harms from the stars of one’s birth, 
The fears that arise from a multitude of actions,
And the disturbances of the elements.
{{milestone:{label:15.18,id:UT22084-089-013-1441}}}tadyathā |{{note:{index:322,id:UT22084-089-013-1442}}} śame viṣame svāhā | sagaṭe vigaṭe svāhā | sukhatinate svāhā | {{page:{number:164,id:UT22084-089-013-3115,folio:F.233.a}}} sāgarasaṃbhūtāya svāhā | skandhamatāya svāhā | nīlakaṇṭhāya svāhā | aparājitavīryāya svāhā | himavatsaṃbhūtāya svāhā | animilavaktrāya svāhā | namo bhagavate brāhmaṇe | namaḥ sarasvatyai devyai sidhyantu mantrapadā daṃ brahma anumanyatu svāhā |{{note:{index:323,id:UT22084-089-013-1443}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.19,id:UT22084-089-013-1444}}}“I will be there, because of this washing ritual, in order to guard the dharmabhāṇaka bhikṣu and those who listen to the Dharma and those who write it out.
{{milestone:{label:15.20,id:UT22084-089-013-1445}}}“Together with a host of devas,{{note:{index:324,id:UT22084-089-013-1446}}} I will end all illness in those villages, towns, marketplaces, and monasteries. 
{{milestone:{label:15.21,id:UT22084-089-013-1447}}}“I will end harm from planetary afflictions, fighting, and pollution; harm from the stars of one’s birth; and all harm from nightmares, troublesome demons, and all evil spirits and vetālas for the bhikṣus, bhikṣuṇīs, upāsakas, and upāsikās who possess this lord of sūtras, so that their lifespans will be benefited, they will abandon saṃsāra, they will progress irreversibly to the highest, most complete enlightenment, and they will quickly attain the highest, most complete enlightenment of buddhahood.”
{{milestone:{label:15.22,id:UT22084-089-013-3221}}}Then the Bhagavat congratulated the great goddess Sarasvatī, saying, “Well done, well done, great goddess Sarasvatī! You act to bring benefit to many beings, and happiness to many beings. It is excellent, excellent that you have given this teaching of mantras and medicines.”
{{milestone:{label:15.23,id:UT22084-089-013-1448}}}The great goddess Sarasvatī bowed down to the Bhagavat’s feet and sat to one side. 
{{milestone:{label:15.24,id:UT22084-089-013-1449}}}Then the Kauṇḍinya brahmin, the Dharma master Vyākaraṇa, called upon the goddess Sarasvatī:
{{milestone:{label:15.25,id:UT22084-089-013-1450}}}“Great goddess Sarasvatī,
You are worthy of offering, a great ascetic;
You are renowned{{note:{index:325,id:UT22084-089-013-1451}}} in all worlds; {{page:{number:165,id:UT22084-089-013-3116,folio:F.233.b}}}
You give the best and have great qualities;{{note:{index:326,id:UT22084-089-013-1452}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.26,id:UT22084-089-013-1453}}}“You have the highest attainment, are beautiful, 
And have put on a darbha grass robe—
You are wearing darbha grass clothing,{{note:{index:327,id:UT22084-089-013-1454}}}
And you stand on one leg. 
{{milestone:{label:15.27,id:UT22084-089-013-1455}}}“All the devas have gathered,
And they all speak in one voice:
‘Loosen your tongue and speak
The words that will benefit beings.’ ”
{{milestone:{label:15.28,id:UT22084-089-013-1456}}}Sarasvatī spoke these mantra words:
{{milestone:{label:15.29,id:UT22084-089-013-1457}}}syād yathedaṃ{{note:{index:328,id:UT22084-089-013-1458}}} mure cire avaje avajavate higule{{note:{index:329,id:UT22084-089-013-1459}}} migule{{note:{index:330,id:UT22084-089-013-1460}}} pigalavati{{note:{index:331,id:UT22084-089-013-1461}}} maguśe{{note:{index:332,id:UT22084-089-013-1462}}} marici samati daśamati agrimagri tara citara{{note:{index:333,id:UT22084-089-013-1463}}} capati{{note:{index:334,id:UT22084-089-013-1464}}} cicirī śirimiri marici praṇaye{{note:{index:335,id:UT22084-089-013-1465}}} lokajyeṣṭhe{{note:{index:336,id:UT22084-089-013-1466}}} lokapriye{{note:{index:337,id:UT22084-089-013-1467}}} siddhiprite{{note:{index:338,id:UT22084-089-013-1468}}} vimamukhiśucikharī{{note:{index:339,id:UT22084-089-013-1469}}} apratihate{{note:{index:340,id:UT22084-089-013-1470}}} apratehata buddhe{{note:{index:341,id:UT22084-089-013-1471}}} namuci namuci mahādevī{{note:{index:342,id:UT22084-089-013-1472}}} pratigṛhnanamaskaraṃ{{note:{index:343,id:UT22084-089-013-1473}}} |{{note:{index:344,id:UT22084-089-013-1474}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.30,id:UT22084-089-013-1475}}}“May I{{note:{index:345,id:UT22084-089-013-1476}}} have unimpeded understanding. May I accomplish the knowledge{{note:{index:346,id:UT22084-089-013-1477}}} of treatises, verses, tantras,{{note:{index:347,id:UT22084-089-013-1478}}} piṭakas, poetry, and so on.
{{milestone:{label:15.31,id:UT22084-089-013-1479}}}tadyathā | mahāprabhavā{{note:{index:348,id:UT22084-089-013-1480}}} hili hili mili mili |{{note:{index:349,id:UT22084-089-013-1481}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.32,id:UT22084-089-013-1482}}}“May I be victorious through the power of the Bhagavatī, the goddess Sarasvatī.
{{milestone:{label:15.33,id:UT22084-089-013-1483}}}karaṭe keyūre keyūravati{{note:{index:350,id:UT22084-089-013-1484}}} hili mili hili mili hili hili |{{note:{index:351,id:UT22084-089-013-1485}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.34,id:UT22084-089-013-1486}}}“I summon the great goddess through the truth of the Buddha, the truth of the Dharma, the truth of the Saṅgha, the truth of Indra, and the truth of Varuṇa. I invoke the great goddess through the truth and true words of all who speak truth in the world.
{{milestone:{label:15.35,id:UT22084-089-013-1487}}}tadyathā | hili hili{{note:{index:352,id:UT22084-089-013-1488}}} hili mili hili mili |{{note:{index:353,id:UT22084-089-013-1489}}} May I be victorious! I pay homage to the Bhagavatī, the great goddess Sarasvatī! May I accomplish the mantra words! svāhā |
{{milestone:{label:15.36,id:UT22084-089-013-1490}}}{{note:{index:354,id:UT22084-089-013-1491}}}Then Sarasvatī said to the Kauṇḍinya brahmin, {{page:{number:166,id:UT22084-089-013-3117,folio:F.234.a}}} “Great being, it is excellent, excellent, that you give all beings excellent eloquence, miracles, higher cognitions, great wisdom, and so on, benefiting them and causing them to quickly attain enlightenment.”
{{milestone:{label:15.37,id:UT22084-089-013-1492}}}She then recited these verses in order to teach the rite of possessing this sūtra:
{{milestone:{label:15.38,id:UT22084-089-013-1493}}}“First, whoever recites this dhāraṇī 
Should pay homage to the Three Jewels.
Then, by repeating it without error,
They will attain excellent accomplishments.
{{milestone:{label:15.39,id:UT22084-089-013-1494}}}“Pay homage to the buddhas, 
The Dharma, the bodhisattvas, 
The pratyekabuddhas, the śrāvakas, 
And to Brahmā, Śakra, and the Four Mahārājas,
{{milestone:{label:15.40,id:UT22084-089-013-1495}}}“And imagine that you reverently serve
Those who continually practice celibacy.
{{milestone:{label:15.41,id:UT22084-089-013-1496}}}“In a place that is peaceful and solitary, 
Recite audibly the dhāraṇīs and praises,
And set out a vast offering
To all the buddhas, devas, and nāgas.
{{milestone:{label:15.42,id:UT22084-089-013-1497}}}“Develop a motivation of compassion 
Toward the many classes of beings.
Contemplate with a one-pointed mind
The Bhagavat’s golden color and his signs.
{{milestone:{label:15.43,id:UT22084-089-013-1498}}}“Contemplate well the words and meaning
Given specifically for individual capacities
Through the Dharma, the supreme speech of the Bhagavat,
And accomplish and remain in emptiness.
{{milestone:{label:15.44,id:UT22084-089-013-1499}}}“If you contemplate with a one-pointed mind
The direct presence of all the bhagavats,
Then you will obtain samādhi, 
Wisdom, and the sublime dhāraṇī. 
{{milestone:{label:15.45,id:UT22084-089-013-1500}}}“The Dharma speech from the glorious throat of the Bhagavat,
That sublime voice, guides his followers. 
His tongue covers the trichiliocosm 
And manifests various, individual wonders.
{{milestone:{label:15.46,id:UT22084-089-013-1501}}}“If you continually contemplate that excellent,
Supreme speech, you will attain fearlessness.
This inconceivable sign of his tongue
Was attained through the power of vast prayers.
{{milestone:{label:15.47,id:UT22084-089-013-1502}}}“Just as space has no impediment,
He teaches that phenomena are nonexistent.
Contemplate the speech of the feature that is the Buddha’s tongue,
And countless prayers will be fulfilled. {{page:{number:167,id:UT22084-089-013-3118,folio:F.234.b}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.48,id:UT22084-089-013-1503}}}“If someone makes offerings to Sarasvatī
Or has a student who, according to instructions,
In accord with scripture, practices the Dharma,
They will obtain the most perfect honors.
{{milestone:{label:15.49,id:UT22084-089-013-1504}}}“Someone who practices for supreme wisdom
And single-mindedly possesses this Dharma
Will increase the accumulations of wisdom and merit
And have definite accomplishment; do not doubt it!
{{milestone:{label:15.50,id:UT22084-089-013-1505}}}“Those who practice for wealth will have wealth,
And gain and fame will likewise be accomplished.
Those who wish for deliverance will be liberated.
This will definitely be accomplished; do not doubt it!
{{milestone:{label:15.51,id:UT22084-089-013-1506}}}“Also numerous, countless good qualities
Will be accomplished, as wished for.
Someone who maintains this practice correctly
Will definitely accomplish them; do not doubt it!
{{milestone:{label:15.52,id:UT22084-089-013-1507}}}“Wear clean clothes in a solitary place,
And in a maṇḍala of whatever size you can make
Place four vases that are extensive.
At that time, offer flowers and incense.
{{milestone:{label:15.53,id:UT22084-089-013-1508}}}“Beautify{{note:{index:355,id:UT22084-089-013-1509}}} it with flags, parasols, and streamers,
And adorn it extensively with ointments and powders.
Make offerings to the buddhas and Sarasvatī,
And if you wish to see that deity, you will see her.
{{milestone:{label:15.54,id:UT22084-089-013-1510}}}“In front of the goddess Sarasvatī
Recite and repeat this for three weeks.
If you still have not seen that deity,
Repeat with a stable mind for nine more days.
{{milestone:{label:15.55,id:UT22084-089-013-1511}}}“If she has not been seen in those nights,
Seek another auspicious place.
Draw a correct image of the goddess 
And continuously offer, repeat, and recite.
{{milestone:{label:15.56,id:UT22084-089-013-1512}}}“Day and night make a continuous effort 
For an immeasurable benefit to yourself and others.
Its result will be bestowed on others
And your wishes will be accomplished.
{{milestone:{label:15.57,id:UT22084-089-013-1513}}}“If in that way your wishes have not been accomplished,
Then for three months, or for six months, or nine,
Or with diligent mantra repetition for a year,
You will attain the six higher cognitions, and so on.”
{{milestone:{label:15.58,id:UT22084-089-013-1514}}}The Kauṇḍinya brahmin, on hearing that teaching, felt immeasurable joy and delight, and he said to that gathered assembly:
{{milestone:{label:15.59,id:UT22084-089-013-1515}}}“This entire assembly of devas, humans, and others, {{page:{number:168,id:UT22084-089-013-3119,folio:F.235.a}}}
Listen to me with undistracted minds.
I will recite these verses 
Based upon relative truth,
In order to praise the supreme goddess Sarasvatī.
{{milestone:{label:15.60,id:UT22084-089-013-1516}}}“I pay homage to the goddess with great power,
Who has attained power over this world realm.
I am going to praise you because 
This has been taught by the ṛṣis of the past.
{{milestone:{label:15.61,id:UT22084-089-013-1517}}}“Your glorious mind possesses bliss and learning
And it is renowned for its beauty.
You are also the mother who gave birth to this world
And continuously acts with great diligence in glory.
{{milestone:{label:15.62,id:UT22084-089-013-1518}}}“You are always victorious on the battleground.
Through subjugation you give rise to compassion and patience, 
You manifest the body of Yama’s sister,
And you always wear clothes of blue silk.
{{milestone:{label:15.63,id:UT22084-089-013-1519}}}“You manifest both beauty and ugliness.
Whoever sees your eyes will have trust in you.
Your immeasurable activity transcends the world.
Whoever comes to you for refuge, you take care of them.
{{milestone:{label:15.64,id:UT22084-089-013-1520}}}“Sometimes you dwell on mountains and rocks,
Sometimes in caves or on riverbanks,
Or also within forests of trees—
Those places are the dwellings of the goddess.
{{milestone:{label:15.65,id:UT22084-089-013-1521}}}“If you continually make offerings to the goddess,
Just as the humans in the borderlands do,
Who make parasols from peacock feathers,
Then she will protect the world at all times.
{{milestone:{label:15.66,id:UT22084-089-013-1522}}}“She is encircled by tigers and lions;
Birds and cattle also depend on her.
When the sound of her great bell resounds
It is heard even on the Vindhya mountains.
{{milestone:{label:15.67,id:UT22084-089-013-1523}}}“In her hands she holds a trident,
Or she holds the sun and moon as her standard.
On the eleventh day of the waning moon,
Or on the ninth, make offerings to her.
{{milestone:{label:15.68,id:UT22084-089-013-1524}}}“Because she looks upon the entire world,
When a battle is being waged, through her kindness,
She manifests as the goddess Vasu. 
She is a supreme goddess beyond analogy.
{{milestone:{label:15.69,id:UT22084-089-013-1525}}}“She manifests the form of the gopi Rādhā,{{note:{index:356,id:UT22084-089-013-1526}}}
And even fighting devas, she is always victorious.
She dwells happily for a long time in the world,
Sometimes wrathful, and sometimes peaceful.
{{milestone:{label:15.70,id:UT22084-089-013-1527}}}“She is skilled in the four Dharmas{{note:{index:357,id:UT22084-089-013-1528}}} that are taught
By the brahmins, and in all miracles and mantras.
She has attained the power of the ṛṣis and devas
And creates this great earth and its seeds. {{page:{number:169,id:UT22084-089-013-3120,folio:F.235.b}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.71,id:UT22084-089-013-1529}}}“Also, when she gathers together goddesses,
They come and gather like ocean waves.{{note:{index:358,id:UT22084-089-013-1530}}}
She is chief among all the assemblies of many yakṣas, nāgas,
And so on, and she has the power to guide them.
{{milestone:{label:15.72,id:UT22084-089-013-1531}}}“She is supreme among all female celibates.
She has power like{{note:{index:359,id:UT22084-089-013-1532}}} a lord of the world.
She is also like a lotus in a royal dwelling
Or like a boat or ship on a river.
{{milestone:{label:15.73,id:UT22084-089-013-1533}}}“Her wide face is like the full moon.
She is a support for scholars.
Her eloquence is as elevated as a mountain peak 
And she reveals a continent of contemplation.
{{milestone:{label:15.74,id:UT22084-089-013-1534}}}“The devas, such as the asuras and so on,
All praise and extol her qualities.
Even thousand-eyed Śakra, the king of devas,
Gazes on her face with veneration.
{{milestone:{label:15.75,id:UT22084-089-013-1535}}}“Whatever it is that beings wish for,
She quickly fulfills all those wishes.
She has a swift mind, retains what she hears,
And is supreme over all on this great earth.
{{milestone:{label:15.76,id:UT22084-089-013-1536}}}“She is always like a great illuminating lamp.
In the world realms within the ten directions
She even fulfills all the wishes of all
Birds, carnivores, and herbivores.
{{milestone:{label:15.77,id:UT22084-089-013-1537}}}“She is like a mountain peak among females;
Like the ṛṣis of the past, she remains for a long time;{{note:{index:360,id:UT22084-089-013-1538}}}
Like a young goddess, she is free of desire,
And she speaks the truth like the Lord of Sahā.
{{milestone:{label:15.78,id:UT22084-089-013-1539}}}“You manifest a body that accords with the world.
You are the chief among goddesses.
Even in the paradises of the desire realm,
There is no being that is greater.
{{milestone:{label:15.79,id:UT22084-089-013-1540}}}“She will save from the dangers
Of battles and dangerous places,
From falling into a pit of fire, 
And from rivers, crevasses, and savages.
{{milestone:{label:15.80,id:UT22084-089-013-1541}}}“Those who are bound in punishment by kings
Or are being killed by an enemy,
If their minds are one-pointed and unwavering, 
They will be freed from that suffering.
{{milestone:{label:15.81,id:UT22084-089-013-1542}}}“You protect all, the good and the bad.
You are present before them with love and affection.
Therefore, in my mind I bow down 
And I pay homage to the great goddess.”
{{milestone:{label:15.82,id:UT22084-089-013-1543}}}{{note:{index:361,id:UT22084-089-013-1544}}}Then the Kauṇḍinya brahmin, the Dharma master Vyākaraṇa, praised the goddess Sarasvatī with these verses: {{page:{number:170,id:UT22084-089-013-3121,folio:F.236.a}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.83,id:UT22084-089-013-1545}}}“All hosts of spirits, listen to me!
I praise the perfectly beautiful face of the sublime goddess,
The sublime female, the highest of perfect goddesses
In the world with its devas, gandharvas, and lords of devas.
{{milestone:{label:15.84,id:UT22084-089-013-1546}}}“The one named Sarasvatī is endowed with vast eyes. 
Her limbs are adorned by an accumulation of various qualities.
She shines with merit, a vastness of stainless wisdom and qualities.
She is like a vision of an accumulation of different jewels.
{{milestone:{label:15.85,id:UT22084-089-013-1547}}}“I praise her, who has the exceptional qualities of supreme speech.
She produces the supreme, sublime accomplishments.
She produces true praises and good qualities.
She is stainlessly supreme, a shining lotus.
{{milestone:{label:15.86,id:UT22084-089-013-1548}}}“She has supreme eyes, sublime eyes.
She is the basis for goodness, a vision of goodness.
She is adorned with inconceivable qualities.
She is like the moon, shining with pure light.
{{milestone:{label:15.87,id:UT22084-089-013-1549}}}“She is the source of wisdom and has sublime memory.
She is a supreme lion, the divine steed of humans.
She is adorned with eight arms{{note:{index:362,id:UT22084-089-013-1550}}}
And she shines like the full moon.
{{milestone:{label:15.88,id:UT22084-089-013-1551}}}She has a beautiful voice and lovely speech.
She is endowed with profound wisdom. 
She is a sublime being who provides the highest needs.
Her abode is praised by all the hosts of deva and asura lords,
And she is continually offered to by the hosts of spirits: svāhā.{{note:{index:363,id:UT22084-089-013-1552}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.89,id:UT22084-089-013-1553}}}“I{{note:{index:364,id:UT22084-089-013-1554}}} pay homage to this goddess.
May she bestow special qualities on me. 
May she grant me the accomplishment of all that is needed.
May she constantly protect me{{note:{index:365,id:UT22084-089-013-1555}}} in the midst of enemies.
{{milestone:{label:15.90,id:UT22084-089-013-1556}}}“In the morning, on arising, recite purely
These complete syllables, the full words,
And all wishes, wealth, and grain will be attained,
And vast accomplishment and goodness will also be obtained.” {{page:{number:171,id:UT22084-089-013-3122,folio:F.236.b}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.91,id:UT22084-089-013-1557}}}The Bhagavat then congratulated the Kauṇḍinya brahmin, saying, “It is excellent, excellent, that you, for the sake of the benefit and happiness of beings, have recited this praise to the goddess Sarasvatī and received sublime accomplishment so that you will possess immeasurable merit.”
{{milestone:{label:15.93,id:UT22084-089-013-1559}}}Then the Kauṇḍinya brahmin, the Dharma master Vyākaraṇa, having prayed to the great goddess Sarasvatī with words of praise and eulogy, said to the assembly, “If you wish to invite the goddess Sarasvatī, be protected by her compassion, have unimpeded eloquence in this life, possess what you have heard, have great wisdom, be skilled in all treatises, and accomplish clear and unimpeded in the adornments of composition, then with a respectful motivation{{note:{index:366,id:UT22084-089-013-1560}}} and a reverential mind recite these words in order to invite the goddess Sarasvatī:
{{milestone:{label:15.94,id:UT22084-089-013-1561}}}“I pay homage to the Buddha.
I pay homage to the Dharma.
I pay homage to the Saṅgha.
{{milestone:{label:15.95,id:UT22084-089-013-1562}}}“I pay homage to the bodhisattvas, śrāvakas, pratyekabuddhas, and all āryas of the past, future, and present.
{{milestone:{label:15.96,id:UT22084-089-013-1563}}}“I rejoice in the speech of the bhagavats in the ten directions who remain in valid true speech, who are without deception, and who speak the teaching of the truth in accord with individual capacities and correctly teach the truth constantly for countless millions of eons.
{{milestone:{label:15.97,id:UT22084-089-013-1564}}}“I bow my body and pay homage to all the bhagavats who, in speaking the truth, spread their vast, long tongues, so that they completely cover their faces, Jambudvīpa, the Four Mahārājas,{{note:{index:367,id:UT22084-089-013-1565}}} a chiliocosm, a dichiliocosm, a trichiliocosm, and all the countless world realms in the ten directions, dispelling all affliction from the defilements. {{page:{number:172,id:UT22084-089-013-3123,folio:F.237.a}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.98,id:UT22084-089-013-1566}}}“May I possess such a sublime sign of the tongue and limitless eloquence.
{{milestone:{label:15.99,id:UT22084-089-013-1567}}}“I pay homage to the supreme eloquence of the Bhagavat; 
To the supreme eloquence of the great bodhisattvas; 
To the supreme eloquence of the ārya pratyekabuddhas; 
To the supreme eloquence of the four pairs and eight individuals; 
{{milestone:{label:15.100,id:UT22084-089-013-1568}}}“To the supreme eloquence of the four truths; 
To the supreme eloquence of the true vision;
To the supreme eloquence of the ṛṣis in Brahmā’s entourage; 
To the supreme eloquence of Umādevī; 
{{milestone:{label:15.101,id:UT22084-089-013-1569}}}“To the supreme eloquence of the deity Skanda; 
To the supreme eloquence of the nāga Manasvin; 
To the supreme eloquence of the goddess of the night; 
To the supreme eloquence of the Four Mahārājas; 
{{milestone:{label:15.102,id:UT22084-089-013-1570}}}“To the supreme eloquence of the devas in paradises; 
To the supreme eloquence of Vajra­guhyakādhipati; 
To the supreme eloquence of the deity Viṣṇu; 
To the supreme eloquence of the goddess Padmā;{{note:{index:368,id:UT22084-089-013-1571}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.103,id:UT22084-089-013-1572}}}“To the supreme eloquence of the deity Ganeśa; 
To the supreme eloquence of the goddess Śrī; 
To the supreme eloquence of the goddess Śrīmatī; 
To the supreme eloquence of Haridhara;{{note:{index:369,id:UT22084-089-013-1573}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.104,id:UT22084-089-013-1574}}}“To the supreme eloquence of all the mātṛkās; 
To the supreme eloquence of Hārītī; 
To the supreme eloquence of the yakṣas; 
To the supreme eloquence of the buddhas; 
And to the supreme eloquence of the jinas in the ten directions.
{{milestone:{label:15.105,id:UT22084-089-013-1575}}}“May I have power through all supreme actions
And attain supreme, infinite eloquence.
{{milestone:{label:15.106,id:UT22084-089-013-1576}}}“I pay homage to the one who is infallible.
I pay homage to the one who is completely liberated.
I pay homage to the one who is free of desire.
I pay homage to the one who has cut through bondage.
{{milestone:{label:15.107,id:UT22084-089-013-1577}}}“I pay homage to the one with a pure mind.
I pay homage to the one who shines with light.
I pay homage to the speaker of true words.
I pay homage to the one who is free of dust.
{{milestone:{label:15.108,id:UT22084-089-013-1578}}}“I pay homage to the one who dwells in the ultimate.
I pay homage to the lord of the great assembly.
I pay homage to the goddess Sarasvatī.
{{milestone:{label:15.109,id:UT22084-089-013-1579}}}“Cause my words to be unimpeded
And swiftly accomplish every one
Of all the aspirations that I have.
May I obtain health, constant happiness,
And also may my lifetime be long. {{page:{number:173,id:UT22084-089-013-3124,folio:F.237.b}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.110,id:UT22084-089-013-1580}}}“Quickly fulfill every aspiration:
Bring skill in all the branches of knowledge,
Bring diligence on the path to enlightenment,
And bring many benefits to all beings.
{{milestone:{label:15.111,id:UT22084-089-013-1581}}}“I speak the genuine words of truth
And I speak infallible words.
May the supreme goddess Sarasvatī
Cause my goals to be accomplished!
{{milestone:{label:15.112,id:UT22084-089-013-1582}}}“I pray, goddess, that you come to this place
And make my words free of impediment.
Quickly enter my body and mouth
And quickly perfect my mind’s eloquence.
{{milestone:{label:15.113,id:UT22084-089-013-1583}}}“Make the faculty of my tongue 
Have the eloquence of the tathāgatas.
Make me be a guide for beings
Through the brilliance and power of my words.
{{milestone:{label:15.114,id:UT22084-089-013-1584}}}“Whatever words there are that I speak,
May all their meanings be accomplished!
May everyone have reverence for my words,
And may all that I do not be wasted.
{{milestone:{label:15.115,id:UT22084-089-013-1585}}}“If when I wish for eloquence
That goal is not accomplished,
Then, goddess, your words of truth 
Will all become nothing but lies.
{{milestone:{label:15.116,id:UT22084-089-013-1586}}}“Those who have created the bad karma with immediate result
Will become guided by the Buddha’s words.
The words of any arhat
And the words of Kṛtajña, 
{{milestone:{label:15.117,id:UT22084-089-013-1587}}}“And the words of truth of those such as
Śāriputra and Maudgalyāyana,
The leaders among the Bhagavat’s followers,
May they all be accomplished by me.
{{milestone:{label:15.118,id:UT22084-089-013-1588}}}“On this day I invite to this place
The Buddha and his assembly of disciples;
May they all quickly come to this place
So that my aspirations will be fulfilled.
{{milestone:{label:15.119,id:UT22084-089-013-1589}}}“When I supplicate with valid words of truth
May they all become infallible.
From the summit of existence down—
Everyone in the Śuddhāvāsa paradises,
{{milestone:{label:15.120,id:UT22084-089-013-1590}}}“In all of the Brahmakāyika, Brahmapurohita, 
And Brahma­pariṣadya paradises, 
Throughout the circle of the trichiliocosm—
The lord of the Sahā world
{{milestone:{label:15.121,id:UT22084-089-013-1591}}}“And all those in his entourage,
All of them I invite here today.
Look upon me with compassion 
And completely take me into your loving care. {{page:{number:174,id:UT22084-089-013-3125,folio:F.238.a}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.122,id:UT22084-089-013-1592}}}“The Paranirmita­vaśavartin devas
And also the Nirmāṇarati devas;
The devas in the sky in Tuṣita,
The dwelling of Maitreya who will be a buddha;
{{milestone:{label:15.123,id:UT22084-089-013-1593}}}“The devas of the Yāma paradise,
The devas of Trāyastriṃśa,
And the devas of the Four Mahārājas;
And also all the assemblies of other devas—
{{milestone:{label:15.124,id:UT22084-089-013-1594}}}“The devas of earth, water, fire, and air;
Those who dwell on Sumeru Mountain,
And devas of the mountains of the seven oceans,
All of them and their entourages;
{{milestone:{label:15.125,id:UT22084-089-013-1595}}}“Pañcaśikha and Vāsuki;
And the sun, moon, planets, and lunar asterisms—
Those and all other devas, and those who are
The source of happiness in the world;
{{milestone:{label:15.126,id:UT22084-089-013-1596}}}“Those and all other devas
Who do not aspire to bad actions;
The mother with reverence for the buddha
Who had love for her youngest son;{{note:{index:370,id:UT22084-089-013-1597}}}
{{milestone:{label:15.127,id:UT22084-089-013-1598}}}“And devas, nāgas, and yakṣas, 
Gandharvas and asuras,
And also the kinnaras,
The mahoragas, and so on—
{{milestone:{label:15.128,id:UT22084-089-013-1599}}}“Today I invite them all of them here 
Through the power of the Bhagavat.
By regarding me with love and compassion,
Develop unimpeded eloquence within me.
{{milestone:{label:15.129,id:UT22084-089-013-1600}}}“May those who know the minds of others,
Those of all the devas and humans,
Through all their power of blessing 
Bestow supreme eloquence upon me.
{{milestone:{label:15.130,id:UT22084-089-013-1601}}}“All of those beings that there are
As far as the end of the element of space,
The limits of the realm of phenomena,
May they bestow upon me supreme eloquence!”
{{milestone:{label:15.131,id:UT22084-089-013-1602}}}After the Kauṇḍinya brahmin said those words to the goddess Sarasvatī, the goddess said to that great being, “Well done! Any noble man or noble woman who praises with those verses and possesses and keeps those mantra words, and goes for refuge to the Three Jewels, and with a focused, aspiring mind practices in accordance with the rite for their desired goal, {{page:{number:175,id:UT22084-089-013-3126,folio:F.238.b}}} this will not be a waste. Moreover, if they possess, keep, read, and recite this extremely subtle and profound Sublime Golden Light, the king that is the lord of sūtras, then all their aspirations will be quickly accomplished, unless this is done with a distracted mind.”
{{milestone:{label:15.132,id:UT22084-089-013-1603}}}At that time, the brahmin, his mind filled with admiration and overjoyed, placed his palms together in acceptance.
{{milestone:{label:15.133,id:UT22084-089-013-1604}}}Then the Bhagavat congratulated the goddess Sarasvatī, saying, “Goddess, it is excellent, excellent, that you protect and spread this sublime Dharma and that you teach this kind of Dharma to all the beings who possess this sūtra, so that happiness, merit, and limitless eloquence increase, and that you cause those who have developed the aspiration to quickly attain the highest, most complete enlightenment.”
{{milestone:{label:15.134,id:UT22084-089-013-1605}}}This concludes “The Goddess Sarasvatī,” the fifteenth chapter of “The Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light.”
{{milestone:{label:16,id:UT22084-089-013-chapter-16}}}Chapter 16: The Great Goddess Śrī 
{{milestone:{label:16.1,id:UT22084-089-013-1607}}}Then the great goddess Śrī said to the Bhagavat, “Venerable Bhagavat, I, the great goddess Śrī, will also, in whatever way, bring a perfection of requisites to those dharmabhāṇaka bhikṣus so that they will gain freedom from deprivation; will have a resolute{{note:{index:371,id:UT22084-089-013-1608}}} mind; will day and night have happiness of mind; will learn, understand, and correctly recite all the different words and letters in this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light so that, for the sake of those beings who have planted good roots with hundreds of thousands of buddhas, this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light{{page:{number:176,id:UT22084-089-013-3127,folio:F.239.a}}} will remain for a long time in Jambudvīpa and will not disappear, and so that beings will experience the happiness of devas and humans for many hundreds of thousands of quintillions of eons, and so that there will be no famine and instead excellent harvests. Beings will become happy through being endowed with every kind of happiness. They will be in the company of tathāgatas, and in some future time they will attain the highest, most complete enlightenment of buddhahood. This will end all the suffering in the hells, in the lives of animals, and in the world of Yama. Robes, food, bedding, medicine while ill, requisites, and other necessities will be brought to those dharmabhāṇaka bhikṣus.
{{milestone:{label:16.2,id:UT22084-089-013-1609}}}“I,{{note:{index:372,id:UT22084-089-013-1610}}} the great goddess Śrī, developed good roots with the tathāgata arhat samyaksaṃbuddha Ratna­kusuma­guṇa­sāgara­vaiḍūrya­kanaka­giri­suvarṇa­kāñcana­prabhāsaśrī. In the present, wherever I direct my mind, wherever I look, wherever I go, many hundreds of thousands of quintillions of beings become happy; they become endowed with every kind of happiness. They do not lack food, drink, wealth, grain, cowries, gold, jewels, pearls, beryl, conchs, crystals, coral, silver, unwrought gold, or other requisites. {{page:{number:177,id:UT22084-089-013-3128,folio:F.239.b}}} Those beings are endowed with all requisites.{{note:{index:373,id:UT22084-089-013-1611}}} Through the power of the great goddess Śrī, they make offerings to that tathāgata. They make offerings of perfumes, flowers, and incense.{{note:{index:374,id:UT22084-089-013-1612}}} They recite the name ‘the great goddess Śrī’{{note:{index:375,id:UT22084-089-013-1613}}} three times, and offer him perfume, incense, and flowers.{{note:{index:376,id:UT22084-089-013-1614}}} They also offer him a variety of flavors, and then their great accumulations of grain increase. It is said concerning this:
{{milestone:{label:16.3,id:UT22084-089-013-1615}}}“The fertility of the earth increases in the earth.
The devas will be constantly, perfectly happy.
The deities{{note:{index:377,id:UT22084-089-013-1616}}} of fruits, harvests, plants, and trees
Cause a great variety of harvests to arise.
{{milestone:{label:16.4,id:UT22084-089-013-1617}}}“I, the great goddess Śrī, will direct my mind toward those beings who say the name of The Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light and I will create a great splendor for them.”
{{milestone:{label:16.5,id:UT22084-089-013-1618}}}Then the Bhagavat congratulated the great goddess Śrī, saying, “It is excellent, excellent that you, goddess, through remembering your past actions make offerings to the tathāgata to benefit countless beings, bring them the benefit of happiness, and possess the inexhaustible merit from spreading this sūtra.”
{{milestone:{label:16.6,id:UT22084-089-013-1619}}}This concludes “The Great Goddess Śrī,” the sixteenth chapter of “The Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light.”
{{milestone:{label:17,id:UT22084-089-013-chapter-17}}}Chapter 17: The Increase of Wealth by the Great Goddess Śrī 
{{milestone:{label:17.1,id:UT22084-089-013-1621}}}Then the great goddess Śrī said these words to the Bhagavat, “Bhagavat, not far from here to the north, in the environs of Alakāvati, the palace of Mahārāja Vaiśravaṇa, there is a sublime pleasure grove by the name of Puṇya­kusuma­prabha, in which there is a mansion made of the seven precious materials which is called Padmottara­suvarṇa­dhvaja,{{note:{index:378,id:UT22084-089-013-1622}}} which is where I live.
{{milestone:{label:17.2,id:UT22084-089-013-1623}}}“Any person who wishes to increase their accumulation of grain {{page:{number:178,id:UT22084-089-013-3129,folio:F.240.a}}} should clean their house well, wash well, wear clean white clothes, wear clothes that have been perfumed, bow down to the tathāgata arhat samyaksaṃbuddha Ratnakusumaguṇasāgaravaiḍūrya-kanakagirivarṇabhadrasuvarṇaprabhāsaśrī, and say his name three times. Then the great goddess Śrī{{note:{index:379,id:UT22084-089-013-1624}}} will make an offering with her own hands. Flowers, incense, and perfume should also be offered. Various kinds of flavors should also be offered. The name of The Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light should be recited three times and words of truth recited. Also, offerings should be made to the great goddess Śrī. When flowers and incense are offered, and various kinds of flavors are offered, at that time, through the power of this Lord King of Sūtras, the great goddess Śrī will turn her mind toward that house and its great accumulation of grain will increase.
{{milestone:{label:17.3,id:UT22084-089-013-1625}}}“Those who wish to invoke the great goddess Śrī should remember these vidyāmantras: 
{{milestone:{label:17.4,id:UT22084-089-013-1626}}}“ ‘I pay homage to all the buddhas of the past, the future, and the present. 
{{milestone:{label:17.5,id:UT22084-089-013-1627}}}“ ‘I pay homage to all the buddhas and bodhisattvas.
{{milestone:{label:17.6,id:UT22084-089-013-1628}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the Bhagavat Tathāgata Ratnaśikhin.
{{milestone:{label:17.7,id:UT22084-089-013-1629}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the Bhagavat Tathāgata Tip of Brilliant, Precious, Pure Fire. 
{{milestone:{label:17.8,id:UT22084-089-013-1630}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the Tathāgata Jambu Golden Victory Banner That is Golden in Appearance. 
{{milestone:{label:17.9,id:UT22084-089-013-1631}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the Tathāgata Suvarṇa­prabhā­garbha. 
{{milestone:{label:17.10,id:UT22084-089-013-1632}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the Tathāgata Radiance of a Hundred Suns’ Illuminating Essence. 
{{milestone:{label:17.11,id:UT22084-089-013-1633}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the Tathāgata Suvarṇa­ratnākaracchatra­kūṭa. {{page:{number:179,id:UT22084-089-013-3130,folio:F.240.b}}}
{{milestone:{label:17.12,id:UT22084-089-013-1634}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the Tathāgata Suvarṇa­puṣpa­jvala­raśmi­ketu. 
{{milestone:{label:17.13,id:UT22084-089-013-1635}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the Tathāgata Mahāpradīpa. 
{{milestone:{label:17.14,id:UT22084-089-013-1636}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the Tathāgata Ratnaketu.
{{milestone:{label:17.15,id:UT22084-089-013-1637}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the Tathāgata Akṣobhya in the east.
{{milestone:{label:17.16,id:UT22084-089-013-1638}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the Tathāgata Ratnaketu in the south.
{{milestone:{label:17.17,id:UT22084-089-013-1639}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the Tathāgata Amitābha in the west.
{{milestone:{label:17.18,id:UT22084-089-013-1640}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the Tathāgata Dundubhisvara in the north.
{{milestone:{label:17.19,id:UT22084-089-013-1641}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the bodhisattva Maitreya.
{{milestone:{label:17.20,id:UT22084-089-013-1642}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the bodhisattva Ruciraketu.
{{milestone:{label:17.21,id:UT22084-089-013-1643}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the bodhisattva Suvarṇa­prabhāsottama. 
{{milestone:{label:17.22,id:UT22084-089-013-1644}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the bodhisattva Golden Essence.
{{milestone:{label:17.23,id:UT22084-089-013-1645}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the bodhisattva Sadāprarudita.
{{milestone:{label:17.24,id:UT22084-089-013-1646}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the bodhisattva Dharmodgata. 
{{milestone:{label:17.25,id:UT22084-089-013-1647}}}“ ‘I pay homage to the bodhisattva Supratiṣṭha.’
{{milestone:{label:17.26,id:UT22084-089-013-1648}}}“Having paid homage to them, I will practice this mantra. 
{{milestone:{label:17.27,id:UT22084-089-013-1649}}}“ ‘This vidyāmantra will bring me wealth: 
{{milestone:{label:17.28,id:UT22084-089-013-1650}}}syād yathedam{{note:{index:380,id:UT22084-089-013-1651}}} pratipūrṇavare samantavedanagate{{note:{index:381,id:UT22084-089-013-1652}}} mahākāryapratiprāpaṇe sattvārtha{{note:{index:382,id:UT22084-089-013-1653}}}samatānuprapūre ayānadharmitāmahābhogine{{note:{index:383,id:UT22084-089-013-1654}}} mahāmaitre{{note:{index:384,id:UT22084-089-013-1655}}} upasaṃhihe{{note:{index:385,id:UT22084-089-013-1656}}} saṃgṛhīte{{note:{index:386,id:UT22084-089-013-1657}}} samarthānupālane{{note:{index:387,id:UT22084-089-013-1658}}} svāhā |
{{milestone:{label:17.29,id:UT22084-089-013-1659}}}“These are words with an infallible meaning. That single-sentence mantra has the nature of an empowerment bestowed upon the crown of the head and bestows the valid accomplishment of the true nature.
{{milestone:{label:17.30,id:UT22084-089-013-1660}}}“The practice for beings of middling capacity is to possess and recite this, while keeping the eight vows for seven years{{note:{index:388,id:UT22084-089-013-1661}}} without transgressions but only roots of merit. {{page:{number:180,id:UT22084-089-013-3131,folio:F.241.a}}} In order for themselves and others to perfect omniscient wisdom, each morning and afternoon they should make offerings of flowers and incense to all the buddhas and pray, ‘May I fulfill this wish of mine, may I fulfill it quickly.’ 
{{milestone:{label:17.31,id:UT22084-089-013-1662}}}“In a temple or in a solitary place, clean the building and make a circle of dung. Offer perfume and incense. Arrange a clean seat, scatter flower petals on the ground and then sit on it. 
{{milestone:{label:17.32,id:UT22084-089-013-1663}}}“Then, in that instant, the great goddess Śrī will come and reside there. From then on, that house, village, town, market town, temple, or place of solitude will never be disturbed and never be in need. Everyone will obtain cowries, gold, jewels, wealth, grain, and all requisites; they will become happy through all that brings happiness.
{{milestone:{label:17.33,id:UT22084-089-013-1664}}}“Whatever good actions have been done, give the supreme part to the great goddess Śrī, and because of that she will remain with you for as long as you live and will never abandon you. All your aspirations will be completely fulfilled.”
{{milestone:{label:17.34,id:UT22084-089-013-1665}}}This concludes “The Increase of Wealth by the Great Goddess Śrī,” the seventeenth chapter of “The Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light.”
{{milestone:{label:18,id:UT22084-089-013-chapter-18}}}Chapter 18: Dṛḍhā, the Goddess of the Earth
{{milestone:{label:18.1,id:UT22084-089-013-1667}}}Then Dṛḍhā, the goddess of the earth, said to the Bhagavat, “Venerable Bhagavat, wherever this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light is taught, in the present or in future times, whether in a village, town, market town, {{page:{number:181,id:UT22084-089-013-3132,folio:F.241.b}}} region, wilderness, mountain cave,{{note:{index:389,id:UT22084-089-013-1668}}} or royal residence—wherever, venerable Bhagavat, this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light is taught at length{{note:{index:390,id:UT22084-089-013-1669}}}—I, Dṛḍhā, the goddess of the earth, will come to that place. 
{{milestone:{label:18.2,id:UT22084-089-013-1670}}}“Wherever a Dharma throne is arranged for the dharmabhāṇaka bhikṣu, and wherever the dharmabhāṇaka, upon that throne, extensively teaches this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light, venerable Bhagavat, I, Dṛḍhā, the goddess of the earth, will come to that place. With my body invisible, I will go beneath that Dharma throne, and with my highest limb, my head, I will support that dharmabhāṇaka bhikṣu under the soles of his feet.
{{milestone:{label:18.3,id:UT22084-089-013-1671}}}“I also will listen to the Dharma and be satiated by this amṛta liquid of the Dharma. I will honor him; I will make offerings to him. Having been satiated, having honored him, and being delighted, I will increase the fertility of this sixty-eight-thousand-yojana-wide aggregation of the earth down to its vajra foundation. I will honor it and perfect it. On its surface I will saturate this disk of the earth, as far as the ocean, with the oil of the earth’s fertility. I will cause this great earth to be resplendent. Then, in this Jambudvīpa, the grass, bushes, herbs, and forests will grow with perfect resplendence. {{page:{number:182,id:UT22084-089-013-3133,folio:F.242.a}}} All parks, forests, trees, leaves, flowers, fruits, and harvests of various kinds will be resplendent, aromatic, lustrous, delicious, beautiful, and huge. 
{{milestone:{label:18.4,id:UT22084-089-013-1672}}}“When beings consume them as various kinds of drink and food, their lifespans, strength, complexions, and faculties will increase. Being endowed with such majesty, strength, complexion, and form, they will accomplish many hundreds of thousands of the various different things necessary on this earth. They will be dedicated to that and make an effort in that. They will accomplish actions that create strength. 
{{milestone:{label:18.5,id:UT22084-089-013-1673}}}“Venerable Bhagavat, that will cause all of Jambudvīpa to have peace, good harvests, increase, and joy. It will become filled with human beings. All the beings in Jambudvīpa will become happy and experience various kinds of joy. Those beings will possess majesty, strength, and excellent color and form. 
{{milestone:{label:18.6,id:UT22084-089-013-1675}}}“For the sake of this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light, bhikṣus, bhikṣuṇīs, upāsakas, and upāsikās should approach the Dharma seat of those who possess this lord and king of the sūtras. Having approached it with a perfectly trusting mind, for the welfare, benefit, and happiness of all beings, they should supplicate the dharmabhāṇaka so that this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light will be taught extensively. {{page:{number:183,id:UT22084-089-013-3134,folio:F.242.b}}}
{{milestone:{label:18.7,id:UT22084-089-013-1676}}}“Why should they do that? Venerable Bhagavat, if this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light is taught, I, the earth goddess Dṛḍhā, with my servants, will have supreme magnificence and supreme strength. Our bodies will develop perfect strength, diligence, and great power. Our bodies will gain magnificence, glory, and splendor. 
{{milestone:{label:18.8,id:UT22084-089-013-1677}}}“Venerable Bhagavat, I, the earth goddess Dṛḍhā, will be satiated by this amṛta liquid of the Dharma. I will attain great magnificence, strength, diligence, power, and speed.{{note:{index:391,id:UT22084-089-013-1678}}} The great fertility of earth will increase in this Jambudvīpa’s seven thousand yojanas. The great earth will become magnificent.
{{milestone:{label:18.9,id:UT22084-089-013-1679}}}“Venerable Bhagavat, the beings who dwell upon the earth will increase, expand, and become vast. They will also become widespread, and just as the beings who are upon the earth will become widespread, they will also experience a variety of enjoyments. They will experience happiness. They will all enjoy various kinds of food and drink, remain in various kinds of happiness with the entire variety of pleasurable requisites that are present upon the earth, appear from the earth, and are dependent upon the earth, such as clothes, beds, seats, dwellings, houses, divine palaces, parks, rivers, pools, springs, ponds, lakes, and reservoirs.
{{milestone:{label:18.10,id:UT22084-089-013-1680}}}“Venerable Bhagavat, because of this, all those beings will be repaying my kindness. There is no doubt that this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light should be respected, {{page:{number:184,id:UT22084-089-013-3135,folio:F.243.a}}} listened to, honored, venerated, revered, and offered to.
{{milestone:{label:18.11,id:UT22084-089-013-1681}}}“Venerable Bhagavat, when those beings leave their individual families and individual homes in order to go to the dharmabhāṇaka; and having gone there have listened to this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light; and having heard it returned to their own individual families, homes, villages, and market towns, they will say to those who live in their own home, ‘We have heard a profound Dharma today. We have obtained an inconceivable accumulation of merit today. By listening to that Dharma, we have pleased many hundreds of thousands of quintillions of tathāgatas. By listening to that Dharma today, we have been completely freed from rebirth in the hells, as animals, in the world of Yama, and in the realm of the pretas. By listening to this Dharma today, we have obtained rebirth in the future as devas and humans for many hundreds of thousands of lifetimes.’
{{milestone:{label:18.12,id:UT22084-089-013-1682}}}“When they are in their own homes, if they tell even one example from this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light to those other beings, or just one chapter from this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light, or one history, or even the name of one bodhisattva, or the name of one tathāgata, or even just one four-line verse, or even a single line of verse, and those other beings hear it—or even if they teach others the name only of this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light—then, venerable Bhagavat, wherever those different beings in different places speak about, or listen to, or talk to one another about these various kinds of causes from the sūtra, then, venerable Bhagavat, {{page:{number:185,id:UT22084-089-013-3136,folio:F.243.b}}} all those places will become very magnificent. They will become very lustrous. In those various places, for all those beings, the various fertilities of the earth and all requisites will increase, augment, and expand, and all those beings will be happy. They will have great wealth and great enjoyments. They will aspire to generosity, and they will have true faith in the Three Jewels.” 
{{milestone:{label:18.13,id:UT22084-089-013-1683}}}When she had spoken, the Bhagavat said to Dṛḍhā, the goddess of the earth, “Goddess of the earth, if any being listens to even one line from this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light, when they pass away from this human world, they will be reborn as a deva in the Trāyastriṃśa paradise or among another class of devas.{{note:{index:392,id:UT22084-089-013-1684}}}
{{milestone:{label:18.14,id:UT22084-089-013-1685}}}“Goddess of the earth, anyone who, in order to make offerings to this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light, beautifully adorns those places, even with just one parasol or one flag or by draping one cloth, then, goddess of the earth, they will dwell in those constantly adorned places, divine aerial palaces made of the seven jewels in the seven paradises{{note:{index:393,id:UT22084-089-013-1686}}} of the desire realm that are perfectly adorned by all adornments. When those beings pass away from this human realm, they will be reborn in those aerial palaces made of the seven jewels, and at that time, goddess of the earth, they will be reborn seven times in each of those aerial palaces made of the seven jewels. {{page:{number:186,id:UT22084-089-013-3137,folio:F.244.a}}} They will experience the inconceivable bliss of the devas.”
{{milestone:{label:18.15,id:UT22084-089-013-1687}}}When the Bhagavat had spoken, the earth goddess Dṛḍhā said to the Bhagavat, “Therefore, venerable Bhagavat, when the dharmabhāṇaka bhikṣu is seated on the Dharma seat, I, the earth goddess Dṛḍhā, will be present in the ground below that Dharma seat. For the sake of those beings who have planted good roots with hundreds of thousands of buddhas, I will make my body invisible and will support that dharmabhāṇaka bhikṣu’s feet with my highest limb, my head, so that this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light will remain for a long time in Jambudvīpa and will not disappear soon; so that beings will hear this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light and will experience the happiness of devas and humans for many hundreds of thousands of quintillions of eons; and so that they will be in the company of tathāgatas and will, in a future time, attain the highest, most complete enlightenment of buddhahood and will become completely free of the suffering of the hells, the lives of animals, and the world of Yama.”{{note:{index:394,id:UT22084-089-013-1688}}}
{{milestone:{label:18.16,id:UT22084-089-013-1689}}}Then the earth goddess Dṛḍhā said, “Bhagavat, I have a mantra essence. It will bring benefit and happiness to all devas and humans. If someone wishes to see me directly; wishes for precious jewels, treasures, and so on; {{page:{number:187,id:UT22084-089-013-3138,folio:F.244.b}}} wishes for a long life without illness through excellent herbs; or wishes to be free of all adversaries and opponents, they should make a circle in a solitary place, wash, wear new clothes, and sit on an arrangement of straw. In front of an image that contains relics or in front of a stūpa that contains relics, make an offering of flowers, incense, and various kinds of food. On the eighth day during the time of the lunar asterism Puṣya, invite me by repeating this dhāraṇī-mantra single-mindedly.
{{milestone:{label:18.17,id:UT22084-089-013-1690}}}“The mantra is: 
{{milestone:{label:18.18,id:UT22084-089-013-1691}}}tadyathā | cili cili curu curu kuru kuru kuṭu kuṭu toṭu toṭu vaha vaha variṣe variṣe svāhā |
{{milestone:{label:18.19,id:UT22084-089-013-1692}}}“Bhagavat, I will come to anyone among the four classes of followers who repeats these mantra words a hundred and eight times in order to invite me.
{{milestone:{label:18.20,id:UT22084-089-013-1693}}}“Moreover, Bhagavat, anyone who seeks to meet me and speak to me, should do the same as in the previous rite and repeat this mantra: 
{{milestone:{label:18.21,id:UT22084-089-013-1694}}}tadyathā | añcani kyalikṣani śiśidhari haha hihi kuruvare svāhā |
{{milestone:{label:18.22,id:UT22084-089-013-1695}}}“Bhagavat, I will come to the one who repeats the words of this mantra and then repeats the previous mantra, and I will definitely fulfill their wishes. 
{{milestone:{label:18.23,id:UT22084-089-013-1696}}}“Whoever wishes to repeat this mantra, in order to protect their body, should first repeat this mantra: 
{{milestone:{label:18.24,id:UT22084-089-013-1697}}}tadyathā | śiri śiri vāśakati tati kuṭṭi pūta pūderi pūderi{{note:{index:395,id:UT22084-089-013-1698}}} tiṭe pati kukuṭi kapacili svāhā |
{{milestone:{label:18.25,id:UT22084-089-013-1699}}}“Bhagavat, when practicing this dhāraṇī-mantra one should apply the mantra to a cord of five colors, tying a knot with each repetition. Having repeated the mantra in that way twenty-one times, tie the cord on to the left upper arm and this will dispel all danger and the body will be protected. {{page:{number:188,id:UT22084-089-013-3139,folio:F.245.a}}} If this mantra is repeated with an undistracted mind, all wishes will be accomplished. These words of mine are infallible. I pray that the Buddha Jewel, the Dharma Jewel, and the Saṅgha Jewel look upon me and regard me.”
{{milestone:{label:18.26,id:UT22084-089-013-1700}}}Then the Bhagavat congratulated the earth goddess Dṛḍhā, saying, “It is excellent, excellent, that through your words of truth you have protected this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light along with the dharmabhāṇakas. Therefore, you also possess an inconceivable accumulation of merit.”
{{milestone:{label:18.27,id:UT22084-089-013-1701}}}This concludes “Dṛḍhā, the Goddess of the Earth,” the eighteenth chapter of “The Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light.”
{{milestone:{label:19,id:UT22084-089-013-chapter-19}}}Chapter 19: Saṃjñeya, the Lord of Yakṣas
{{milestone:{label:19.1,id:UT22084-089-013-1703}}}Then the great yakṣa general Saṃjñeya, accompanied by twenty-eight yakṣa generals, rose from his seat and with his robe over one shoulder, kneeling with his right knee on the ground and with palms together, bowed toward the Bhagavat and said to the Bhagavat, “Venerable Bhagavat, wherever this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light appears, in the present or in future times, whether in a village, town, market town, region, wilderness, mountain cave,{{note:{index:396,id:UT22084-089-013-1704}}} or royal residence, Bhagavat, I, the great yakṣa general Saṃjñeya, accompanied by twenty-eight yakṣa generals, will come to that village, town, market town, region, wilderness, mountain cave,{{note:{index:397,id:UT22084-089-013-1705}}} or royal residence.
{{milestone:{label:19.2,id:UT22084-089-013-1706}}}“I will make my body invisible and will guard that dharmabhāṇaka bhikṣu. I will defend him, {{page:{number:189,id:UT22084-089-013-3140,folio:F.245.b}}} take care of him, protect him, save him from punishment, and bring him peace and well-being.
{{milestone:{label:19.3,id:UT22084-089-013-1707}}}“All men, women, boys, or girls who listen to the Dharma, whoever hears and retains even one four-line verse from this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light, or even one line, or even the name of one bodhisattva from this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light, or the name of one tathāgata, or even hears and retains just the name of this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light, I will defend them all, take care of them, protect them,{{note:{index:398,id:UT22084-089-013-1708}}} save them from punishment,{{note:{index:399,id:UT22084-089-013-1709}}} and bring them peace and well-being. I will defend, take care of, protect, save from punishment, and bring peace and well-being to all those families, those homes, those villages, those towns, those market towns, those wildernesses, and those royal residences.
{{milestone:{label:19.4,id:UT22084-089-013-1710}}}“Venerable Bhagavat, why am I called the great yakṣa general Saṃjñeya?{{note:{index:400,id:UT22084-089-013-1711}}} Venerable Bhagavat, it is because I know all Dharmas, I understand all Dharmas, I comprehend all Dharmas. Whatever the number of Dharmas, the nature of the Dharmas, or the classes{{note:{index:401,id:UT22084-089-013-1712}}} of Dharmas, venerable Bhagavat, I have direct knowledge of all Dharmas.
{{milestone:{label:19.5,id:UT22084-089-013-1713}}}“Venerable Bhagavat, {{page:{number:190,id:UT22084-089-013-3141,folio:F.246.a}}} in all Dharmas my illumination by wisdom is inconceivable, my clarity{{note:{index:402,id:UT22084-089-013-1714}}} of wisdom is inconceivable, my activity of wisdom is inconceivable, and my accumulation of wisdom is inconceivable.
{{milestone:{label:19.6,id:UT22084-089-013-1715}}}“Venerable Bhagavat, in all Dharmas my engagement in the field of wisdom is inconceivable.
{{milestone:{label:19.7,id:UT22084-089-013-1716}}}“Venerable Bhagavat, it is because of my correct knowledge, my correct examination, my correct view, and my correct comprehension of all Dharmas that I am named the great yakṣa general Saṃjñeya.
{{milestone:{label:19.8,id:UT22084-089-013-1717}}}“Venerable Bhagavat, I will bring eloquence to the dharmabhāṇaka bhikṣu in order to beautify his words. I will bring brilliance to his pores and develop in his body great power, strength, and diligence; I will make the illumination of his wisdom inconceivable; and I will make his memory comprehensive and make him greatly enthusiastic, so that the dharmabhāṇaka’s body will not become fatigued, his body’s faculties will be blissful, he will feel great joy, and so that for the sake of those beings who have planted good roots with hundreds of thousands of buddhas, this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light will remain for a long time in Jambudvīpa and will not soon vanish, and so that beings will hear this Lord King of Sūtras, the Sublime Golden Light and will attain an inconceivable accumulation of wisdom, will possess an accumulation of merit, and in the future will experience inconceivable happiness among devas and humans for many hundreds of thousands of quintillions of eons, will be in the company of tathāgatas, will in a future time attain the highest, most complete enlightenment of buddhahood, and will cease to experience the suffering of the hells, {{page:{number:191,id:UT22084-089-013-3142,folio:F.246.b}}} of birth as animals, or of the world of Yama.”{{note:{index:403,id:UT22084-089-013-1718}}}
{{milestone:{label:19.9,id:UT22084-089-013-1719}}}Saṃjñeya, the great yakṣa general, then said, “Bhagavat I have a dhāraṇī-mantra and through compassion and for the benefit of beings I will recite this mantra in the presence of the Bhagavat.
{{milestone:{label:19.10,id:UT22084-089-013-1720}}}“The mantra is: 
{{milestone:{label:19.11,id:UT22084-089-013-1721}}}namo buddhāya | namo dharmāya | namaḥ saṃghāya | namo brahmāya | nama indrāya | namaś caturnāṃ mahārājānāṃ | tadyathā | hili hili mili mili gauri mahāgauri gandhari mahāgandhari drimiḍi mahādrimiḍi daṇḍakhukhunti haha haha hihi hihi huhu huhu halodhame gudhame caca caca cici cici cucu cucu caṇḍeśvara śikhara śikhara atiṣṭhāhe{{note:{index:404,id:UT22084-089-013-1722}}} bhagavān saṃvidjñāya{{note:{index:405,id:UT22084-089-013-1723}}} svāhā |
{{milestone:{label:19.12,id:UT22084-089-013-1724}}}“I will bestow on anyone who possesses and keeps this vidyāmantra all the requisites of life, alms, clothing, flowers, fruits, wealth, jewels, and so on.
{{milestone:{label:19.13,id:UT22084-089-013-1725}}}“Anyone who wishes for requisites such as sons and daughters, male and female slaves, gold, silver, jewels, adornments, and so on, I will bestow them according to their individual wishes. 
{{milestone:{label:19.14,id:UT22084-089-013-1726}}}“Because this mantra possesses great power and majesty when it is repeated, I will quickly come there and accomplish anything without impediment. 
{{milestone:{label:19.15,id:UT22084-089-013-1727}}}“In the rite for practicing this mantra, first paint an image of Saṃjñeya, the great general of the yakṣas, {{page:{number:192,id:UT22084-089-013-3143,folio:F.247.a}}} four or five hands{{note:{index:406,id:UT22084-089-013-1728}}} in height, holding an axe in his hands. In front of that, make a square maṇḍala and in its four corners place four vases filled with liquid honey or molasses, and make offerings with ointments, powders, burning incense, and flower garlands. Alternatively, dig a fire-offering pit in front of the maṇḍala and in a fire that has no smoke burn a mixture of butter and mustard seeds, making a fire offering with each repetition of the mantra. In that way, make a burnt offering a hundred and eight times. I will reveal my body there and ask the mantra practitioner,{{note:{index:407,id:UT22084-089-013-1729}}} ‘What is it that you want? Tell me what it is that you desire!’ and I will give them whatever they desire. If someone wishes for gold or silver, or wishes to search for treasure, or wishes to be a divine ṛṣi, it will be accomplished and they will attain the ability to fly in the sky and moreover all the higher cognitions, such as divine sight and knowing the minds of others. They will gain as wished for power over all beings and they will end the continuum of all the kleśas and will attain liberation.”
